Description of Problem: Hello, my name is Jonathan Solymos, and I live at 18722 Sloane Avenue in Lakewood. I have an at home job as a livestreamer. What this means is that I will play games on my computer or gaming consoles, and project them live for people to watch. As you know, there are some people out there who are out to be as mean as possible to others, for whatever reason, and there are people who try to find out the personal information of people in a situation like myself. Unfortunately, through some database leaks, someone has found out some personal information about me, such as my full name and home address. There is an unfortunate trend that goes on called 'SWATing' that people do to streamers once their information gets leaked. What it entails is basically, someone calls in to the country sheriff or local authorities, and acts like the residence of the streamer has some type of hostage situation or bomb threat, or something of the like, which makes the SWAT team raid that person's house, while they are livestreaming, with their webcam on. The SWAT team busts into their house, points guns at their face, as is their job, since they are responding to what they think is a hostile situation, and causes a lot of trouble for both the streamer and the authorities. I honestly doubt that someone would do this to me, as no other personal attacks have been made, and very few attempts have been made to steal my identity, but it is a possibility, and I wanted to make you aware of it ahead of time.
